# Ranking the Best Tara Strong Movies and TV Shows of All Time

![Tara Strong Movies And TV Shows](https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/8Z86FfWbnUJnyFTcLa9MpVVFhMh.jpg)

Canadian-American actress Tara Strong has built an impressive career spanning live-action performances, voice acting roles, and business ventures. Best known to audiences for her work in animated series like The Fairly OddParents and The Powerpuff Girls, Strong has also left her mark on television through her memorable character portrayals in shows like Rugrats and Big Time Rush. This roundup article showcases the depth and versatility that has defined her work in the entertainment industry.

## 1. [Ice Age](https://serp.ly/amazon/Ice+Age)

![Ice Age](https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/gLhHHZUzeseRXShoDyC4VqLgsNv.jpg)

They came. They thawed. They conquered.

<br>

In their icy world, Manny the woolly mammoth, Diego the saber-toothed tiger, and Sid the giant sloth encounter a human baby who has lost its parents. Determined to reunite the orphan with its family, the prehistoric trio embarks on a perilous journey through frozen landscapes and deadly encounters. As they face unimaginable challenges, an unlikely alliance forms between the mighty mammoth, the fierce tiger, and the gentle sloth. Their selfless quest tests the very limits of friendship and courage, revealing the depth of compassion that lies within their prehistoric hearts.
